LIGGGHTS (Version LIGGGHTS-PUBLIC 3.8.0, compiled 2026-05-30-04:17:57 by root, git commit 3d5c00f20519e6bb6eb6756f51f1ad36564e649d)
###################################Header for General commands#######################################################

atom_style	granular		#Simulation of particles

boundary	f f f			#fixed boundaries -> particles will be deleted if leaving the simulation box

units		si

communicate	multi vel yes		#default

newton		off			#default


###################################System variables##################################################################

#Definition of boundaries

variable xmin equal -0.02
variable xmax equal 0.43

variable ymin equal -0.02
variable ymax equal 0.06

variable zmin equal -0.02
variable zmax equal 0.07

#Definition of the timestep

variable dt equal 1e-6



###################################Specific variables for current simulation#########################################

variable natoms equal 2 				#1 -> particle #2 ->pipe and screw

####variable for material properties####

####Young Modulus####
variable	youngmodulus1	equal 	7e6
variable	youngmodulus2	equal 	2e8

####Poission ratio####
variable 	poission1	equal	0.30
variable 	poission2	equal	0.29

####variable for contact properties####

####coefficient of restitution####
variable	CoR11	equal	0.4
variable	CoR12	equal	0.5
variable	CoR21	equal	0.5
variable	CoR22	equal	0.45

####sliding friction coefficient####
variable	sf11	equal	0.65	#Particle-particle sliding friction coefficient
variable	sf12	equal	0.5
variable	sf21	equal	0.5
variable	sf22	equal	0.0


####rolling friction coefficient####
variable	rf11	equal	0.75	#Particle-particle rolling friction coefficient
variable	rf12	equal	0.6
variable	rf21	equal	0.6
variable	rf22	equal	0.0


####variable for particle####

#Number of particle radius
variable	nradii	equal	3

variable	radius1	equal	0.00005	#m
variable	radius2	equal	0.00005	#m
variable	radius3	equal	0.00005	#m

variable	frac1	equal	0.3945
variable	frac2	equal	0.4059
variable	frac3	equal	0.1996

variable	density	equal	280		#kg/m³


####filling parameters####

variable	filltime	equal	2.0		#s, prueba rápida: alimentar 2 s

variable	dischargetime	equal	100		#s, tiempo para que puedan salir partículas

variable	fillmass	equal	4.4e-8 		#kg, 2 g de material

variable	fillmassrate	equal	${fillmass}/${filltime}	#kg/s
variable	fillmassrate	equal	4.4e-08/${filltime}	
variable	fillmassrate	equal	4.4e-08/2	

variable	fillsteps	equal	${filltime}/${dt}
variable	fillsteps	equal	2/${dt}
variable	fillsteps	equal	2/1e-06

variable	dischargesteps	equal	${dischargetime}/${dt}
variable	dischargesteps	equal	100/${dt}
variable	dischargesteps	equal	100/1e-06



####screw velocities####

variable	screwPeriod	equal	1.029		#s, prueba rápida: 2 vueltas/s



###################################Definition of simulationbox#######################################################

region		reg block ${xmin} ${xmax} ${ymin} ${ymax} ${zmin} ${zmax} units box
region		reg block -0.02 ${xmax} ${ymin} ${ymax} ${zmin} ${zmax} units box
region		reg block -0.02 0.43 ${ymin} ${ymax} ${zmin} ${zmax} units box
region		reg block -0.02 0.43 -0.02 ${ymax} ${zmin} ${zmax} units box
region		reg block -0.02 0.43 -0.02 0.06 ${zmin} ${zmax} units box
region		reg block -0.02 0.43 -0.02 0.06 -0.02 ${zmax} units box
region		reg block -0.02 0.43 -0.02 0.06 -0.02 0.07 units box

processors 6 1 1

create_box	2 reg
Created orthogonal box = (-0.02 -0.02 -0.02) to (0.43 0.06 0.07)
  6 by 1 by 1 MPI processor grid


neighbor	0.0001 bin

neigh_modify	delay 0


#################################Definition of the contact models####################################################

pair_style gran model hertz tangential history rolling_friction epsd2

pair_coeff	* *

timestep ${dt}
timestep 1e-06

thermo 10000

fix		integrator all nve/sphere

fix		gravi all gravity 9.81 vector 0.0 0.0 -1.0


###################################Definition of Material properties#################################################

fix 		m1 all property/global youngsModulus peratomtype ${youngmodulus1} ${youngmodulus2}
fix 		m1 all property/global youngsModulus peratomtype 7000000 ${youngmodulus2}
fix 		m1 all property/global youngsModulus peratomtype 7000000 200000000

fix 		m2 all property/global poissonsRatio peratomtype ${poission1} ${poission2}
fix 		m2 all property/global poissonsRatio peratomtype 0.3 ${poission2}
fix 		m2 all property/global poissonsRatio peratomtype 0.3 0.29

fix 		m3 all property/global coefficientRestitution peratomtypepair ${natoms} ${CoR11} ${CoR12} ${CoR21} ${CoR22}
fix 		m3 all property/global coefficientRestitution peratomtypepair 2 ${CoR11} ${CoR12} ${CoR21} ${CoR22}
fix 		m3 all property/global coefficientRestitution peratomtypepair 2 0.4 ${CoR12} ${CoR21} ${CoR22}
fix 		m3 all property/global coefficientRestitution peratomtypepair 2 0.4 0.5 ${CoR21} ${CoR22}
fix 		m3 all property/global coefficientRestitution peratomtypepair 2 0.4 0.5 0.5 ${CoR22}
fix 		m3 all property/global coefficientRestitution peratomtypepair 2 0.4 0.5 0.5 0.45

fix 		m4 all property/global coefficientFriction peratomtypepair ${natoms} ${sf11} ${sf12} ${sf21} ${sf22}
fix 		m4 all property/global coefficientFriction peratomtypepair 2 ${sf11} ${sf12} ${sf21} ${sf22}
fix 		m4 all property/global coefficientFriction peratomtypepair 2 0.65 ${sf12} ${sf21} ${sf22}
fix 		m4 all property/global coefficientFriction peratomtypepair 2 0.65 0.5 ${sf21} ${sf22}
fix 		m4 all property/global coefficientFriction peratomtypepair 2 0.65 0.5 0.5 ${sf22}
fix 		m4 all property/global coefficientFriction peratomtypepair 2 0.65 0.5 0.5 0

fix 		m5 all property/global coefficientRollingFriction peratomtypepair ${natoms} ${rf11} ${rf12} ${rf21} ${rf22}
fix 		m5 all property/global coefficientRollingFriction peratomtypepair 2 ${rf11} ${rf12} ${rf21} ${rf22}
fix 		m5 all property/global coefficientRollingFriction peratomtypepair 2 0.75 ${rf12} ${rf21} ${rf22}
fix 		m5 all property/global coefficientRollingFriction peratomtypepair 2 0.75 0.6 ${rf21} ${rf22}
fix 		m5 all property/global coefficientRollingFriction peratomtypepair 2 0.75 0.6 0.6 ${rf22}
fix 		m5 all property/global coefficientRollingFriction peratomtypepair 2 0.75 0.6 0.6 0



###################################Generation and Loading of the Geometry .stl#######################################
fix case all mesh/surface file case_remesh.stl type 2 heal auto_remove_duplicates scale 1.0 curvature 1e-5 curvature_tolerant yes

fix screw all mesh/surface file screw_simplified.stl type 2 scale 1.0 curvature 1e-5 curvature_tolerant yes

fix 		walls 		all wall/gran model hertz tangential history rolling_friction epsd2 mesh n_meshes 2 meshes case screw

fix		Movescrew	all move/mesh mesh screw rotate origin 0.2024435 0.019051 0.011497 axis -1. 0. 0. period ${screwPeriod}
fix		Movescrew	all move/mesh mesh screw rotate origin 0.2024435 0.019051 0.011497 axis -1. 0. 0. period 1.029

fix feed all mesh/surface file feed.stl type 2 scale 1.0 curvature 1e-5 curvature_tolerant yes

fix outlet all mesh/surface file outlet_1.stl type 2 scale 1.0 curvature 1e-5 curvature_tolerant yes


###################################Generation and Insertion of the particles#########################################

fix pts1 all particletemplate/sphere 10487 atom_type 1 density constant ${density} radius constant ${radius1} volume_limit 1e-18
fix pts1 all particletemplate/sphere 10487 atom_type 1 density constant 280 radius constant ${radius1} volume_limit 1e-18
fix pts1 all particletemplate/sphere 10487 atom_type 1 density constant 280 radius constant 5e-05 volume_limit 1e-18

fix pts2 all particletemplate/sphere 11887 atom_type 1 density constant ${density} radius constant ${radius2} volume_limit 1e-18
fix pts2 all particletemplate/sphere 11887 atom_type 1 density constant 280 radius constant ${radius2} volume_limit 1e-18
fix pts2 all particletemplate/sphere 11887 atom_type 1 density constant 280 radius constant 5e-05 volume_limit 1e-18

fix pts3 all particletemplate/sphere 16561 atom_type 1 density constant ${density} radius constant ${radius3} volume_limit 1e-18
fix pts3 all particletemplate/sphere 16561 atom_type 1 density constant 280 radius constant ${radius3} volume_limit 1e-18
fix pts3 all particletemplate/sphere 16561 atom_type 1 density constant 280 radius constant 5e-05 volume_limit 1e-18

fix 		pdd1 all particledistribution/discrete 32452867 ${nradii} pts1 ${frac1} pts2 ${frac2} pts3 ${frac3}
fix 		pdd1 all particledistribution/discrete 32452867 3 pts1 ${frac1} pts2 ${frac2} pts3 ${frac3}
fix 		pdd1 all particledistribution/discrete 32452867 3 pts1 0.3945 pts2 ${frac2} pts3 ${frac3}
fix 		pdd1 all particledistribution/discrete 32452867 3 pts1 0.3945 pts2 0.4059 pts3 ${frac3}
fix 		pdd1 all particledistribution/discrete 32452867 3 pts1 0.3945 pts2 0.4059 pts3 0.1996

fix		ins_mesh all mesh/surface/planar file feed.stl type 1 scale 1.0

fix 		ins all insert/stream seed 15485863 distributiontemplate pdd1         	mass ${fillmass} massrate ${fillmassrate} overlapcheck yes all_in yes vel constant 0 0 -0.03         	insertion_face ins_mesh extrude_length 0.015
fix 		ins all insert/stream seed 15485863 distributiontemplate pdd1         	mass 4.4e-08 massrate ${fillmassrate} overlapcheck yes all_in yes vel constant 0 0 -0.03         	insertion_face ins_mesh extrude_length 0.015
fix 		ins all insert/stream seed 15485863 distributiontemplate pdd1         	mass 4.4e-08 massrate 2.2e-08 overlapcheck yes all_in yes vel constant 0 0 -0.03         	insertion_face ins_mesh extrude_length 0.015


################################### Particle Residence Time Track#########################################

fix 	rt_outlet	all massflow/mesh mesh outlet vec_side 0 0 -1 file rt_outlet.txt writeTime

fix 	rt_inlet	all massflow/mesh mesh feed vec_side 0 0 -1 file rt_inlet.txt writeTime


###################################Outlet mass flow track#########################################

fix	mfout	all massflow/mesh mesh outlet vec_side 0 0 -1

fix	mfin	all massflow/mesh mesh feed vec_side 0 0 -1


variable 	time equal step*dt

variable 	in_mass_flow equal	f_mfin[3]

variable 	out_mass_flow equal	f_mfout[3]

fix mass_flow_rate all print 5000 "${time},${in_mass_flow},${out_mass_flow}" screen no title "t,in_mass_flow,out_mass_flow" file massflow.csv

###################################Dumping of the data for post-processing to visualize############################

#fix ts_check all check/timestep/gran 1000 0.1 0.1

shell 	mkdir -p post

variable dumptime equal 0.2		#guarda cada 0.05 s

variable dumpstep equal ${dumptime}/${dt}
variable dumpstep equal 0.2/${dt}
variable dumpstep equal 0.2/1e-06

dump	dmpparticle all custom ${dumpstep} post/particles_*.liggghts id type x y z vx vy vz fx fy fz radius mass
dump	dmpparticle all custom 200000 post/particles_*.liggghts id type x y z vx vy vz fx fy fz radius mass

dump_modify	dmpparticle sort id

dump	dmpscrew	all	mesh/stl ${dumpstep} post/screw_*.stl screw
dump	dmpscrew	all	mesh/stl 200000 post/screw_*.stl screw


####################################RUN the simulation filling and discharge###########################################################

run	${fillsteps}
run	2000000
